## 4. PI processing map (every field, where plaintext exists, where ciphertext exists, what crosses what boundary, retention)

| Field                                                           | Class                     | Plaintext location             | Ciphertext location                      | Crosses       | Retention                  | Purpose (PIPEDA Principle 2)                                             |
| --------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------- | ------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------- | ------------- | -------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| `users.id`                                                      | C1                        | DB, browser, JWT, audit_log    | n/a                                      | B1, B2        | Membership + 24mo          | Identifier; required for RLS auth.uid()                                  |
| `users.display_name`                                            | C2                        | DB, browser                    | DB at rest AES-256                       | B1, B2        | Membership + 24mo          | UX (greeting, attribution in audit-log labels)                           |
| `users.off_employer_contact`                                    | C2                        | DB, browser                    | DB at rest AES-256                       | B1, B2        | Membership + 24mo          | Channel for co-chair to reach member outside work (invite + emergencies) |
| `users.identity_pubkey`                                         | C1                        | DB, browser, peers             | n/a (public by definition)               | B1, B2        | Membership + 24mo          | Wrap target for committee key                                            |
| `users.identity_privkey_recovery_blob`                          | C2 (ciphertext of secret) | n/a                            | DB                                       | B2            | Membership + 24mo          | Identity-key recovery on device loss                                     |
| IndexedDB: `ident_priv_wrapped_local`                           | C3 (wraps the priv)       | n/a (wrapped)                  | Personal device IndexedDB                | B4            | Until user wipes / removed | Local fast-path decrypt                                                  |
| `committee_membership.role[]`, `.active`                        | C1                        | DB, browser, audit_log         | n/a                                      | B1, B2        | Membership + 24mo          | RLS, role-based UI                                                       |
| `committee_key.public`                                          | C1                        | DB, browser                    | n/a                                      | B1, B2        | Membership + 24mo          | Sealed-box encryption target                                             |
| `committee_key.wrap` (per member)                               | C3                        | n/a                            | DB                                       | B2            | Membership + 24mo          | Member-scoped key delivery                                               |
| `concerns.title_ct` / `.body_ct`                                | C3                        | Browser RAM only               | DB, backup                               | B2            | 7y post-closure            | Concern content (OHSA s.9(18))                                           |
| `concerns.source_name_ct`                                       | C4                        | Browser RAM on reveal only     | DB, backup                               | B2 (NEVER B3) | 7y post-closure            | Identity of complainant; reprisal-sensitive (s.50)                       |
| `concerns.hazard_class`, `.severity`, `.location_id`, `.status` | C1                        | DB, browser, audit_log         | n/a                                      | B1, B2        | 7y post-closure            | Triage and reporting                                                     |
| `inspections.notes_ct`                                          | C3                        | Browser RAM only               | DB, backup, IndexedDB queue (ciphertext) | B2            | 7y                         | Inspection record (s.9(26))                                              |
| Storage: inspection photos                                      | C3                        | Browser RAM only               | Supabase Storage, backup                 | B2            | 7y                         | Inspection evidence                                                      |
| `minutes.draft_body_ct`                                         | C3                        | Browser RAM only               | DB                                       | B2            | 90 days post-finalization  | Worker-side deliberation; privileged                                     |
| `minutes.final_body_ct`                                         | C3                        | Browser RAM (decrypt + render) | DB, backup, **exported PDF (cross B3)**  | B2, B3        | 7y                         | Joint record (s.9(21))                                                   |
| `recommendations.body_ct`                                       | C3                        | Browser RAM                    | DB, backup, **exported PDF (cross B3)**  | B2, B3        | 7y                         | s.9(20)                                                                  |
| `recommendations.employer_response_ct`                          | C3                        | Browser RAM                    | DB, backup                               | B2            | 7y                         | Captured response from employer                                          |
| `reprisal_log.body_ct`                                          | C4                        | Browser RAM on reveal only     | DB, backup                               | B2 (NEVER B3) | Active matter + 7y         | s.50 evidence                                                            |
| `work_refusal.notes_ct`                                         | C4                        | Browser RAM on reveal only     | DB, backup                               | B2 (NEVER B3) | Active matter + 7y         | s.43 evidence                                                            |
| `s51_evidence.*_ct`                                             | C4                        | Browser RAM on reveal only     | DB, backup, Storage                      | B2 (NEVER B3) | Active matter + 7y         | s.51 evidence                                                            |
| `training_records.evidence_ct`                                  | C2                        | Browser RAM                    | DB                                       | B2            | Membership + 24mo          | Certified-member proof                                                   |
| `audit_log.actor_id, action, target_id, prev_hash, ts`          | C1                        | DB, browser                    | n/a (NOT E2EE)                           | B1, B2        | 24mo                       | Tamper-evident accountability                                            |

**Fields that do NOT exist (data minimization):** SIN, DOB, home address, employer name, job title, IP in app logs, geolocation by default.

**Cross-border flows:** None for PI in normal operation. **Sentry EU** receives scrubbed metadata only (ADR-0010); **Supabase + AWS ca-central-1** are US-incorporated but data is in Canada and C3/C4 is ciphertext (ADR-0001). Both are documented and flagged per `.context/constraints.md` rule 4.

---

## 5. Breach-notification trigger map (PIPEDA s.10.1)

PIPEDA s.10.1: notify OPC + affected individuals when a breach creates **real risk of significant harm** (RROSH). Record-keeping for all breaches regardless of severity: **24 months**. See `playbooks/incident-response.md` for response steps.

| Data class                        | Example breach scenario                                                                                                                      | RROSH?                                                                                                                              | Notify OPC?                                                       | Notify individuals?                                                          | Time-to-notify                                                 | Response anchor                                                         |
| --------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| C0 Public                         | Document-library content exfiltrated                                                                                                         | No                                                                                                                                  | No                                                                | No                                                                           | n/a                                                            | n/a                                                                     |
| C1 Operational metadata           | Audit log dumped (subpoena or A5 leak): timestamps, action verbs, user IDs (UUIDs), prev_hash chain. Reveals who-acted-when but not content. | **Sometimes** — for a JHSC, the fact that a worker U accessed reprisal_log at time T can itself be reprisal-precipitating evidence. | Yes (precautionary)                                               | Yes — every active member                                                    | "As soon as feasible" — within 5 business days of confirmation | playbooks/incident-response.md §2 (Notification) + §4 (Coercion/duress) |
| C2 Worker-side PI                 | `users.display_name` + `off_employer_contact` leaked from DB at rest (provider admin or backup-key compromise)                               | **Yes** — combined with the fact that these are JHSC member contacts in an OHSA s.50 context, RROSH is met                          | Yes                                                               | Yes — affected members                                                       | ASAP, target <72h                                              | playbooks/incident-response.md §2                                       |
| C3 Sensitive worker content       | (Practically unreachable) — would require E2EE break OR committee-key compromise + ciphertext exfil                                          | **Yes** — concerns, hazards, draft minutes, inspections, recommendations                                                            | Yes                                                               | Yes — affected members AND originating workers (if identifiable)             | ASAP, target <48h                                              | playbooks/incident-response.md §3 (E2EE failure)                        |
| C4 Highest sensitivity            | (Practically unreachable per C3 rationale plus per-record key) — reprisal log, s.43 notes, s.51 evidence, source_name                        | **Yes — always**                                                                                                                    | Yes                                                               | Yes — including potentially-identified non-app workers if a source was named | ASAP, target <24h                                              | playbooks/incident-response.md §3 + §4                                  |
| Auth credentials (passkeys, TOTP) | Passkey enrollment table exfiltrated (no password equivalents); TOTP secrets exfiltrated mid-enrollment                                      | C2 effective — phishing-resistant by design, but TOTP misuse is possible if intercepted pre-passkey                                 | Yes if any TOTP secret confirmed exfiltrated and not yet consumed | Yes if TOTP secrets implicated                                               | ASAP, target <72h                                              | playbooks/incident-response.md §5 (Auth)                                |

**PHIPA-adjacent note:** Plan §3.1 treats injury/exposure data (s.51 evidence; some reprisal entries about health-causing reprisal) as PHIPA-grade. We do not have a Health Information Custodian, so PHIPA does not technically apply — but the **60-day notification window** is held as the _outer_ limit; we target faster per PIPEDA RROSH. If scope ever expands to a custodian relationship, PHIPA layer is triggered and ADR is required.

**Crypto-shred as containment:** For C3/C4, the primary containment for "ciphertext exfiltrated + we still hold the key" is **key rotation** (destroy old wraps, rotate committee key); for "ciphertext exfiltrated + key compromised", containment is "the data is irreversibly disclosed" — recovery is legal + member notification. The incident-responder playbook owns the decision tree.

---

## 6. Verification of the seven E2EE invariants (ADR-0003)

Each invariant is restated, mapped to a test, and (where applicable) strengthened.

### Invariant 1 — Server never sees a private key in the clear

**Restated:** Identity privates exist client-side or as ciphertext-on-server. Committee data privates exist only as wrapped blobs.
**Testable as written?** Mostly. Strengthen to include negative test against telemetry channel.
**Strengthened mitigation:** _"For every Edge Function and every Supabase function-log entry produced during the test suite, assert no byte sequence matches the format of an unsealed libsodium private key (32-byte high-entropy block in a context labeled `priv`/`secret`/`key`). Active assertion: T07 fixture inserts a known-canary 32-byte 'private-key-shape' value via DevTools into client state, triggers a flow; canary must never appear in any captured server-side log or Sentry payload."_ Tests: T07-test-1.

### Invariant 2 — No "admin recovery"

**Restated:** No server-side mechanism to recover a forgotten passphrase + lost device.
**Testable as written?** Yes, but the test is mostly an "absence" test (no endpoint exists).
**Strengthened mitigation:** _"Route inventory test (CI): no route under `/api/_`exists that accepts (user_id, request_admin_recovery) and returns plaintext identity material. No Edge Function accepts a passphrase-bypass token. Test: attempt to call hypothetical`/api/admin/recover-identity`and`/api/admin/decrypt-as`; assert 404. Manual: documentation explicitly states 'no admin recovery'."\* Tests: T07-test-2.

### Invariant 3 — No plaintext caching server-side, including in Edge Functions

**Testable as written?** Yes — combine with F-09.
**Strengthened mitigation:** as F-09; plus _"Semgrep rule bans `console._(req)`, `console._(req.body)`, `console._(payload)` in Edge Function modules; runtime fixture posts a known-canary plaintext to an Edge Function; capture Supabase function logs; assert canary absent."\* Tests: T07-test-3.

### Invariant 4 — All encryption is libsodium primitives

**Testable as written?** Yes.
**Strengthened mitigation:** _"Semgrep rule: bans `crypto.subtle`, `node:crypto`, `bcrypt`, `aes-_`imports outside`src/lib/crypto/`; allowlists `libsodium-wrappers`only. CI test: full repo`grep -r` for forbidden imports; assert clean. Test: drop a forbidden import in a side branch; assert CI fails."\* Tests: T07-test-4.

### Invariant 5 — Key material in URLs is forbidden

**Testable as written?** Yes.
**Strengthened mitigation:** _"Semgrep rule: bans URL query params named `key`, `secret`, `passphrase`, `priv`, `nonce`; bans `Location: ...?...key=` patterns; bans setting cookies with names matching key patterns. Runtime test: spider every route; assert no URL contains base64-shaped 32+ byte tokens in query strings."_ Tests: T07-test-5.

### Invariant 6 — Rotation is atomic

**Testable as written?** Yes (mapped F-04, F-05).
**Strengthened mitigation:** as F-04 and F-05 combined. **PLUS: handle backup-window forward-secrecy gap (F-06) as an _accepted_ residual, documented in §7.** Tests: T07-test-6a (concurrent rotation), T07-test-6b (X's wrap deleted), T07-test-6c (session revoke same transaction).

### Invariant 7 — C4 records require a second decrypt step logged in the audit log

**Testable as written?** Yes, but original wording is loose ("require a second decrypt step logged"). Tighten:
**Strengthened mitigation:** _"Reading a C4 row writes a `sensitive.read` audit-log entry BEFORE the plaintext is returned to the client (server-side enforcement via SECURITY DEFINER view or Edge Function indirection). Test: SELECT a C4 row directly with a valid member JWT; assert the SELECT either (a) returns the ciphertext and the read is server-instrumented to log on retrieval, OR (b) is funneled through a view/function that requires a logging step. Assert the audit-log row appears within the same transaction as the read."_ **FINDING (cross-link F-33):** original wording invites client-cooperative logging. Tighten to require server-side enforcement. Tests: T07-test-7 + T13-test-3.

### Additional invariant to add — Invariant 8 (proposed): Key-material mutation audit trail

**Proposed wording:** _"Every mutation of key material (committee_key insert/update; wrap insert/delete; rotation) emits an audit-log row with a defined enum action and hash-chains to the prior audit row."_ Justification: F-07 surfaced this gap. **HUMAN-GATE DECISION:** add Invariant 8 to ADR-0003 (lightweight ADR amendment) before T07 ships.

---

## 7. Open threats / accepted risks (v1)

Each item has a documented rationale and a follow-up.

| ID   | Open threat                                                                                                                                                                                                | Rationale                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Follow-up                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| ---- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| O-1  | **Duress mode / plausible deniability** (F-41) — coerced rep coerced to log in and surrender data                                                                                                          | Locked v2 per plan §13 item 5 and §14. v1 mitigation: visible audit-log + post-coercion notification (T11/T18).                                                                                                                   | Track in `KNOWN-GAPS.md`; revisit Phase 3 or later.                                                                                                                                         |
| O-2  | **Backup-window forward-secrecy gap** (F-06) — removed member could decrypt OLD ciphertext from a dump dated before removal IF backup-key AND their identity key are both available                        | Accepted as the price of having an off-Supabase ciphertext copy at all (ADR-0012).                                                                                                                                                | Document explicitly in privacy policy; tighten 35-day window if cost permits.                                                                                                               |
| O-3  | **Browser DevTools / heap dump** (F-11, F-23) — anyone with local browser access sees plaintext in memory                                                                                                  | Cannot mitigate in a PWA; out of scope. Session hygiene (15-min lock) bounds the window.                                                                                                                                          | Onboarding copy warns; consider native shells in v2 only if T2 risk profile changes.                                                                                                        |
| O-4  | **Co-chair-and-author collusion** (F-31) — author edits own reprisal entry with co-chair's blessing                                                                                                        | Author + co-chair both within trust circle by design.                                                                                                                                                                             | Visible sensitive-activity feed; relies on social norms.                                                                                                                                    |
| O-5  | **Personal-device installation on employer device** (T2 residual)                                                                                                                                          | Locked advisory posture (ADR-0008); no MDM detection.                                                                                                                                                                             | Track installs that warn the user; onboarding nudges; v2 may add WebAuthn attestation review.                                                                                               |
| O-6  | **Email channel for TOTP invite intercepted** (F-38 residual)                                                                                                                                              | TOTP is single-use, short-lived; paper-slip alternative exists.                                                                                                                                                                   | Document; co-chair offers paper as default.                                                                                                                                                 |

| O-11 | **Offline-queue HMAC integrity** (F-44)                                                                                                                                                                    | Not in any ADR.                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | **Add to T10**.                                                                                                                                                                             |
| O-12 | **Key-material mutation audit-log enum** (F-07)                                                                                                                                                            | Not in audit-log spec.                                                                                                                                                                                                            | **Add to T07 + T18** (ADR-0003 Invariant 8 proposal).                                                                                                                                       |
| O-13 | **List-payload exclusion of source_name** (F-18)                                                                                                                                                           | Not explicit in T08 acceptance.                                                                                                                                                                                                   | **Add to T08**.                                                                                                                                                                             |
| O-14 | **C4 server-side enforced read-audit** (F-33, Invariant 7)                                                                                                                                                 | Original wording client-cooperative.                                                                                                                                                                                              | **Tighten T13**.                                                                                                                                                                            |
| O-15 | **Bucket Object Lock for backups** (F-49)                                                                                                                                                                  | Not in ADR-0012.                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | **Add to T17**.                                                                                                                                                                             |
| O-16 | **Reprisal-log status-flip as soft-delete** (F-36)                                                                                                                                                         | Not gated by 4-eyes today.                                                                                                                                                                                                        | **Add to T13**.                                                                                                                                                                             |
| O-17 | **Protected-modal focus-trap timing ambiguity** (F-53, a11y A-2)                                                                                                                                           | Design-system §3.1/§3.2 do not pin trap-engagement to `modal.show()`. Coercion-resistance posture (RA-1 compensating controls) is timing-sensitive.                                                                               | **Architect amendment pass #2** to tighten §3.1/§3.2 wording; test-writer to land M-53a/b/c invariants regardless. If RA-1 / HG-1 lands as single-signer, M-53a/b/c become launch-blockers. |
| O-18 | **Recovery-passphrase low-vision escape hatch** (F-54, a11y A-5)                                                                                                                                           | Surface D.6 currently has only "fail 3 times to re-display" path; punitive for low-vision / dyslexia / cognitive-impairment users. Audio-narration mode rejected (widens threat space); hold-to-reveal + cap + audit-log adopted. | **Add to T07 + design-system §4.D**; new audit-log enum value `identity_privkey.recovery_blob.viewed`; en-CA plain-language strings required.                                               |
| O-19 | **Panic-wipe local-only residual** (F-106 / F-109 / F-115; §8.T19 panic-wipe residual block) — un-revoked server sessions, off-device JSON-blob theft, and HTTP-cache flush gaps survive a local-only wipe | User-adjudicated 2026-05-24 (Q4 disposition: local-only v1). Surface H (D.5) is the user-driven path for server-side session revocation; panic-wipe modal copy guides the user to also visit Sessions when safe.                  | Tracked as G-T19-3 in `.context/known-gaps.md` (server-cascade panic-wipe is a future task with its own threat-modeler re-pass).                                                            |

## 8. Mitigations the test-writer must convert to failing tests

Grouped by task. Each is a one-line, testable assertion derived from §3.

### T00 — Scaffold

- (none specific to threat model beyond standard verify.sh)

### T01 — Supabase + region

- _Region pin: project metadata returns `ca-central-1`; CI fails on any other region._ (ADR-0001)

### T02 — Observability

- _PI canary test: known canary string submitted to a form does not appear in captured Sentry payload._ (T9, ADR-0010)
- _Semgrep: ban `Sentry.captureException(err, { extra: { ... } })` with non-allowlisted keys._ (ADR-0010)

### T04 — Schema + RLS

- _Every table has RLS enabled (relrowsecurity=true)._ (ADR-0004)
- _Helper functions (is_active_member, is_co_chair, is_certified_member, is_self) exist and are SECURITY DEFINER owned by `migration_role`._ (ADR-0004, F-14)
- _Audit-log table is append-only at the DB level: UPDATE/DELETE revoked for all roles except retention-job role._ (T18)

### T05 — Auth + session

- **F-37 / T7:** _Passkey RP-ID is the production eTLD+1; assertion from `evil.example.ca` and `jhsc-example.com` fails with NotAllowedError._
- **F-38:** _TOTP bootstrap: single-use, <=15min validity, <=5 attempts/15min/user; consumed atomically with passkey enrollment._
- **F-39:** _Server-side jti revocation: JWT replayed after revoke-all returns 401 within 5 seconds and remains 401 for the JWT's TTL._
- **F-40 / T8:** _Auth response for unknown vs wrong-credential is byte-identical and timing-equivalent within 50ms._
- **F-42:** _Auth rate limit: <=10 WebAuthn attempts/min/user; 11th returns 429 with no user-enumerating body._
- **F-43:** _After first passkey binds, TOTP row is deleted in the same transaction; subsequent TOTP login attempt returns 401._

### T06 — Committee + invite

- **F-13:** _Non-co-chair UPDATE on `committee_membership.role` denied by RLS (positive + 2 negative tests across worker_member, certified_member)._
- _Co-chair cannot remove themselves without another co-chair's approval (4-eyes)._
- _Single-tenancy: no `committee_id` parameter in any API surface (CI inventory test)._

### T07 — E2EE core

- **F-01:** _Wrap insert for inactive or non-existent member is denied by RLS._
- **F-02:** _Identity-key enrollment requires a self-test unseal of a server-issued nonce; mismatch rolls back the row._
- **F-03:** _Session start runs an IndexedDB identity-key self-test against a server sentinel; failure forces recovery flow and emits `client.identity_selftest_fail`._
- **F-04:** _Concurrent committee-key rotations serialize via Edge Function advisory lock; one succeeds, the other returns 409 within lock TTL; no mixed-state observable._
- **F-05:** _After member removal, removed member's wrap row is absent in `committee_key` AND `committee_key_history`._
- **F-07 (Invariant 8 proposal):** _Every key-material mutation emits an audit-log row with action ∈ {key.committee.create, key.wrap.add, key.wrap.delete, key.committee.rotate} hash-chained._
- **F-08:** _Argon2id parameters meet floor (ops>=4, mem>=512MB or documented per-user floor); per-attempt brute-force >250ms on CI hardware._
- **F-09 / Invariant 3:** _Canary plaintext through every Edge Function emits no plaintext in Supabase function logs or Sentry._
- **F-12:** _Recovery-blob upload: one POST per user; second returns 409 unless reset_recovery is co-chair-issued._
- **F-54 / M-54a (hold-to-reveal):** _Surface D.6 'show passphrase again' control: normal click (release <100ms) does NOT reveal the passphrase in the DOM; sustained pointer-down OR Space-keydown OR Enter-keydown for ≥1500ms reveals; release hides within 50ms._
- **F-54 / M-54b (audit-log emission on reveal):** _Every successful reveal emits one `identity_privkey.recovery_blob.viewed` audit-log row BEFORE the passphrase becomes visible in the DOM with `{actor_id, enrollment_session_id, reveal_count_in_session, ts}`; if the audit-log endpoint returns 500, the passphrase is NOT rendered and a danger toast appears; reveal-count increments per row._
- **F-54 / M-54c (per-enrollment-session cap of 3):** _Three reveals succeed in one enrollment session; fourth attempt: control is aria-disabled, no audit row, helper directs to restart enrollment; restart resets the counter for the new session id._
- **F-54 / M-54d (no TTS, no clipboard on reveal):** _D.6 reveal state contains no clipboard-copy element; static lint: zero matches for `SpeechSynthesisUtterance`, `window.speechSynthesis`, `tts` in recovery-flow modules outside test fixtures._
- **F-54 audit-log enum extension:** _`identity_privkey.recovery_blob.viewed` is a defined enum value in the audit-log action set, recognized by the integrity-checker (F-50) and the retention job (F-51/F-52); reviewers in T15/T18 verify the en-CA plain-language string per a11y-review B-3 contract._
- **Invariant 1 strengthened:** _Canary 32-byte 'private-key-shape' value injected into client state never appears in any server-side log or Sentry payload._
- **Invariant 2 strengthened:** _Route inventory: no `/api/admin/recover-_`or`/api/admin/decrypt-as` route exists; calls to such paths return 404.\*
- **Invariant 4 strengthened:** _Semgrep bans non-libsodium crypto imports outside `src/lib/crypto/`._
- **Invariant 5 strengthened:** _No URL query parameter named `key|secret|passphrase|priv|nonce` exists across the route map._
- **T1 ciphertext shape:** _Every C3/C4 column contains libsodium-shaped ciphertext; admin-connection read does not yield plaintext._

### T08 — Concern intake

- **F-15:** _Non-active-member INSERT on `concerns` denied by RLS (active vs inactive vs no-row)._
- **F-16:** _UPDATE on `concerns` emits audit-log with `prev_field_hashes` for changed fields._
- **F-17:** _Audit log always carries `actor_id` regardless of anonymous-source toggle._
- **F-18:** _Default list payload omits `source_name_ct`; reveal requires explicit query flag + per-record passphrase; reveal writes audit row before plaintext returns._
- **F-20:** _Rate limit on concern create: <=20/hour/user, <=200/24h/user; 21st returns 429._
- _Route inventory: no public POST route exists._ (ADR-0007)
- _Anonymous toggle defaults ON (T3)._

### T09 — Hazard register

- _Severity, location, owner are unencrypted C1 metadata — privacy-reviewer signoff captured._
- _All edits audit-logged._

### T10 — Inspections / offline / photos

- **F-10:** _Service worker cache contains no `/api/_` response that returned C3 content; allowlist enumerable.\*
- **F-44:** _Queue entries carry HMAC keyed by session-derived device key; tampered entries rejected on sync._
- **F-45:** _On session end, IndexedDB holds only ciphertext + passkey-wrapped privkey + public metadata; no plaintext field._
- **F-46:** _EXIF metadata stripped from photos before encryption; both pre-encryption and post-decryption checks confirm no EXIF._
- **F-47:** _Queue capped at 500 items; overflow surfaces warning._
- _Inspection completable fully offline; GPS off by default._

### T11 — Minutes + export

- **F-19 (LAUNCH BLOCKER):** _Export allowlist is a closed const; ESLint forbids spread-into-export-payload outside the allowlist module; PDF text never contains a source_name string; every C4 field is absent from every export allowlist._
- **F-22:** _Non-co-chair GET on finalized minutes ciphertext is denied by RLS (403)._
- **F-24:** _Audit-log POST succeeds before Blob URL is created; mock-fail causes user-visible error and no download._
- **F-25:** _No server route returns `application/pdf`; semgrep enforces._
- **F-27:** _Allowlist hash in audit log matches the hash of the rendering module at runtime; tamper triggers `export.integrity_fail`._
- **F-28:** _Export rate limit: <=10/co-chair/hour; 11th returns 429._
- **F-29 / O-8 (human-gate):** _Either (A) export requires only co-chair passkey re-auth with `approver_id = actor_id`, OR (B) export requires a second active member's passkey assertion with distinct approver_id; same-actor approval rejected with 403._
- **F-53 / M-53a (trap-on-mount):** _With opacity transition extended to 1000ms, a synthesized keydown:Enter at t=10ms after `modal.show()` on the export interstitial does NOT trigger the primary action; document.activeElement is inside the modal; no audit-log row written; scrim catches pointer events from t=0; same test for Escape (cancel path) and click-on-backdrop (no-op for the five protected modals)._
- **F-53 / M-53b (announce-before-input):** _With the `ready` promise stubbed to resolve after 200ms, keydown:Enter at t=10ms does NOT fire the primary handler (button is aria-disabled or handler awaits ready); at t=210ms it does fire; for `export_interstitial` specifically, no `export.minutes` audit-log row and no Blob URL is created if confirm happens before `ready`._
- **F-53 / M-53c (underlying inert from t=0):** _During the transition, programmatic `.focus()` on an underlying-surface button does NOT move activeElement; dispatched keydown:Enter against the underlying button does NOT fire its handler; pointer click at underlying coordinates is captured by the scrim._

### T12 — Recommendations + 21-day timer

- _21-day clock starts on `sent` action; reminders at days 14/18/21._
- _Same export posture as T11 (F-19, F-22, F-24, F-25, F-27, F-28, F-29)._

### T13 — Reprisal log

- **F-30:** _Session invalidation propagates within 5 seconds of `committee_membership.active = false`._
- **F-31:** _UPDATE on `reprisal_log` emits `prev_field_hashes` AND surfaces in 'recent sensitive activity' within 60 seconds._
- **F-32:** _DELETE requires `pending_destructive_ops` row with two distinct approver_ids; same co-chair self-approve denied; success produces two audit rows hash-chained._
- **F-33 / Invariant 7 strengthened:** _Server-side instrumented `sensitive.read` audit row written within the same transaction as the SELECT; bypass via direct SQL still triggers the row._
- **F-34:** _Per-record passphrase is a UX gate only; cryptographic gate is ck_priv; wrong-passphrase attempts emit `sensitive.access_attempt` AND do not reveal plaintext._
- **F-35:** _Rate limit on reprisal_log INSERT: <=10/user/hour._
- **F-36 / O-16:** _Status-flips to {deleted, redacted, tombstoned} on `reprisal_log` are gated by the same 4-eyes flow as DELETE._
- **F-53 (passphrase_prompt variant):** _M-53a/b/c invariants verified for the `passphrase_prompt` modal on Surface C: trap-on-mount, announce-before-input, underlying-inert; passphrase verification handler does NOT fire on confirm before `ready` resolves; no `sensitive.access_attempt` row written for a pre-ready synthesized keydown._
- _Access restricted to author + co-chair + certified_member; positive + negative role tests._

### T14 — Work refusal + s.51

- **F-21:** _Non-certified member SELECT/INSERT/UPDATE on `work_refusal`, `s51_evidence` denied by RLS._
- _All notes are C4; same per-record key + sensitive-read pipeline as T13._

### T15 — Training records + library + reminders

- _Reminders contain no PI; only deep-link into app._

### T16 — Right of access / correction / deletion + retention job

- **F-51:** _Retention-job dry-run is the test default; live run alerts if would-delete > 20 rows._
- **F-52:** _Each retention-job run emits exactly one `retention.pass` audit row with per-table deleted_count and hash-chains._
- _Right of access produces a JSON bundle decrypted in browser; deletion is real delete or crypto-shred._

### T17 — Backup + restore

- **F-06 (accepted residual):** _Backup is ciphertext-of-ciphertext: `pg_dump` file is opened with a random key; decrypt fails._
- **F-48:** _Bucket contains no file whose contents match the dump-key shape; weekly CI sweep asserts._
- **F-49 / O-15:** _Bucket has Object Lock (governance, 35d) and versioning ON; overwriting an existing object creates a new version; deletion under retention denied._
- _Quarterly restore drill produces a signed report._

### T18 — Audit-log integrity + sensitive-read notification

- **F-50:** _Integrity check runs daily + on every committee-key rotation + on every export; corruption alerts within 5 minutes of any of these triggers._
- **F-07 / Invariant 8 proposal:** _Audit-log enum supports key-material mutations._
- _T11 sensitive-read notification surfaces to all active members._

### T19 — Session revocation + panic wipe + onboarding

- **F-39:** as in T05; revocation tested again in panic-wipe context.
- _Panic wipe clears IndexedDB; subsequent navigation requires fresh enrollment or sign-in._
- _Onboarding copy reviewed by tech-writer + privacy-reviewer._
- **F-53 (destructive_confirm variant):** _M-53a/b/c invariants verified for the panic-wipe `destructive_confirm` modal: synthesized keydown:Enter on the WIPE-typed confirm button before `ready` resolves does NOT trigger the wipe; the literal-phrase ("WIPE") input field is also gated by `ready` — its `onChange` does NOT consume input until ready. Synthesized Escape during the transition does NOT dismiss (consistent with §3.2 "no Escape dismiss" for this variant)._
- **F-54 onboarding linkage:** _Surface D.6 must implement the M-54a/b/c/d invariants before T19 ships, since T19 owns the onboarding handoff; an integration test exercises the full D.1→D.7 flow including a 'show again' invocation and verifies the audit-log row appears under the partially-enrolled user._

---

## 9. Required human-gate decisions

These cannot be auto-resolved and need explicit user / co-chair / lawyer sign-off before the relevant task ships.

1. **HG-1 (before T11) — 4-eyes on export (O-8 / F-29).** Decide whether v1 ships with single-signer (co-chair passkey re-auth only) OR true 4-eyes (a second active member's passkey assertion required). Recommendation from threat-modeler: **ship 4-eyes for `recommendations.export` and `minutes.final` exports** — the export is rare, low-friction, and the threat profile (employer adversary, single co-opted co-chair) is exactly what 4-eyes mitigates. Single-signer if 4-eyes is determined operationally infeasible with a single active co-chair.
2. **HG-2 (before T07) — ADR-0003 amendment adding Invariant 8 (F-07 / O-12).** Lightweight ADR amendment documenting the key-material mutation audit-log enum. Architect to draft; user to ratify.
3. **HG-3 (before T10) — ADR addendum on service-worker plaintext cache policy (F-10 / O-10).** Architect to draft an addendum / new ADR specifying the service-worker allowlist; user to ratify.
4. **HG-4 (before T10) — Offline-queue integrity (F-44 / O-11).** Architect to specify HMAC scheme for queue entries; user to ratify before T10 design.
5. **HG-5 (before T10) — EXIF strip mandate on photo uploads (F-46 / O-9).** Add to T10 acceptance; no ADR change required, but flag for designer + implementer.
6. **HG-6 (before T13) — C4 server-side read-audit enforcement (F-33 / O-14, Invariant 7 strengthen).** Architect to amend T13 spec to require server-side enforcement (SECURITY DEFINER view or Edge Function indirection), not client-cooperative logging.
7. **HG-7 (before T13) — Soft-delete-as-delete pattern (F-36 / O-16).** Architect to add status-flip-to-removed gating to T13.
8. **HG-8 (before T17) — Object Lock on backup bucket (F-49 / O-15).** Architect/deployer to enable Object Lock; track in `SUBPROCESSORS.md` and the backup playbook.
9. **HG-9 (already in plan §13.D) — Retention schedule final approval.** Unchanged from architect; called out here because the breach-notification map (§5) presumes the schedule lands.
10. **HG-10 (already in plan §13.B/C) — Privacy lawyer + labour lawyer review** of (a) this threat model + (b) the worker/employer boundary export design + (c) PIPEDA s.10.1 breach map. Must happen before Phase 3 ship.
11. **HG-11 (before T11 — _interacts with HG-1_) — Protected-modal trap-engagement contract (F-53 / O-17 / a11y A-2).** Architect amendment pass #2 must tighten design-system §3.1 and §3.2 to require focus-trap engagement, `aria-modal` / `aria-labelledby` announcement, Escape-handler binding, click-outside no-op binding, AND `inert` on the underlying surface ALL synchronous with `modal.show()`, regardless of opacity-transition state. Add: "announce-on-open `ready` promise gates primary/secondary action handlers." If HG-1 lands as **single-signer** re-auth on export, HG-11 invariants M-53a/b/c are **launch-blockers** (a CI regression on any of them blocks ship); if HG-1 lands as **4-eyes**, M-53a/b/c are still required but the launch-block threshold drops to "high-severity bug, fix before ship". User to ratify the contract; architect to land the §3.1/§3.2 edits.
12. **HG-12 (before T07 / before Surface D ships — _interacts with a11y A-5_) — Recovery-passphrase "show again" surface (F-54 / O-18).** Decide whether v1 lands the hold-to-reveal accommodation per A-5 with the M-54a/b/c/d invariants, OR defers the accommodation and accepts that low-vision / dyslexic / cognitively-impaired users will encounter the "fail 3 times to re-display" punitive path. **Threat-modeler recommendation: land the accommodation in v1.** Justification: (a) the threat-space widening is bounded (enrollment session only, hold-to-reveal, 3-cap, audit-logged); (b) the AODA + WCAG accessibility commitment in `JHSC-APP-PLAN.md` §9 + `.context/constraints.md` AODA section is a hard constraint, not aspirational; (c) the alternative paths (audio narration, second device) were considered and rejected for stronger reasons (audio widens threat space; second device is BYOD-MDM-adjacent). Add `identity_privkey.recovery_blob.viewed` to the audit-log enum. Architect/designer to land Surface D.6 secondary-link spec; test-writer to land M-54a/b/c/d.

No new cross-border transfers introduced by this threat model. The two existing flagged transfers (Sentry EU; Supabase + AWS ca-central US-incorporated) are unchanged.

**For the user — required human-gate decisions before Phase 2 build:** see §9 items HG-1 through HG-8 (HG-9 and HG-10 are pre-existing pre-launch gates; HG-11 and HG-12 are new second-pass items from a11y A-2 and A-5).
